# =========================================================================
# German compound words that are usually not written as 
# separate words.
# Encoding: UTF-8
# All words must contain at least one hyphen or blank,
# even if the word is usually not spelled with a hyphen or blank.
# "+" at the end of the line will turn off the suggestion that
# uses a hyphen.
# "?" at the end of the line will turn off the suggestion that
# uses a hyphen and offers lower-cased joined suggestions.
# "*" at the end of the line will only suggest hyphenated words.
# "$" at the end of the line will allow the hyphenated and non-
# hyphenated variants, but will suggest a lower-cased non-hyphenated
# variant
# \d+ will be expanded to any sequence of digits (e.g., 1, 234, 4543)
#     that are limited by '-' on lines ending on *
# To remove duplicates from this file, use (note: will also remove delimiter lines,
# so restore those before committing):
#     awk -i inplace '!visited[$0]++' this_file
# ==========================================================================
# words that can be written either with or without hyphen (add "$" at the
# end so that the non-hyphenated variant uses lower-cased compounds):
# ===========================================================================
